Editorial note

Curated release posture

The PEMFC release guarantees structural completeness, but generated definitions and retained local vocabulary terms should still be curated by domain experts before claiming full conceptual maturity.

  • The download links in this page target the generated publication tree directly, so they work before any `w3id` namespace registration.
  • The canonical IRI table still records the intended stable public contract for later redirect registration.
  • The schema, curated vocabulary, and examples remain published as separate modules by design.
